    def test_dgo_Grinder_Direction(self, dgo, log, testsuite):
        testCase = "test_dgo_Grinder_Direction"
        time.sleep(2)
        self.result = {}
        myConf = self._getMyConf(testsuite, testCase)
        current_GMT = time.gmtime()
        timeBegin = calendar.timegm(current_GMT)
        self.result["timeBegin"] = timeBegin
        self.result["test"] = testCase
        if myConf.__contains__("retryCount") and myConf.__contains__("retryPeriod"):
            count = 0
            for i in range(myConf["retryCount"]+1):
                count += 1
                _, contrData = dgo.exec_cmd(myConf["command"])
                self.result["cmd"] = myConf["command"]
                self.result["cmd"] = myConf["checkbiDirectional"]
                checkReverse = None
                log.info("    Checking directions in progressing ...")
                if contrData[0][1] == myConf["checkbiDirectional"][0][0] and \
                    contrData[0][3] == myConf["checkbiDirectional"][1][0]:
                    checkReverse = dgo.isReversed(myConf["command"], myConf["checkbiDirectional"][0][0], myConf["checkbiDirectional"][2][0])
                else:
                    checkReverse = dgo.isReversed(myConf["command"], myConf["checkbiDirectional"][0][0], myConf["checkbiDirectional"][1][0])
    
                if checkReverse:
                    log.info("### %s ==> %s", testCase, result.passed)
                    self.result["result"] = result.passed
                    assert True
                    break
                else:
                    if count <= myConf["retryCount"]:
                        log.info("   retrying... %s", count)
                        self.result["retry"] = count
                        time.sleep(myConf["retryPeriod"] / myConf["retryCount"])
                    else:
                        log.info("??? timeout... %s ==> %s", testCase, result.failed)
                        self.result["result"] = result.timeouted
                        dgo.summaries["tests"].append(self.result)
                        assert False
        else:
            _, contrData = dgo.exec_cmd(myConf["command"])
            self.result["cmd"] = myConf["command"]
            self.result["cmd"] = myConf["checkbiDirectional"]
            checkReverse = None
